[30;1m100 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m101 | [0m[35m* **PEM** (Privacy Enhanced Mail) defined in RFC 1421.[0m
[30;1m102 | [0m[35m  In essence PEM files are just base64 encoded versions of the DER encoded data.[0m
[30;1m103 | [0m[35m  In order to distinguish from the outside what kind of data is inside the DER[0m
[30;1m104 | [0m[35m  encoded string, a header and footer are present around the data.[0m
[30;1m105 | [0m[35m[0m
